contact him:- rumblefish1972@hotmail.com<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> In some games (with others to follow) if you receive your game report formatted as a PDF file and like to view<L.31.1>
it on-screen, then click the bookmarks tab (on the left of the display) and you should get some bookmarks to help you get around<L.31.1>
the report more easily. Please try it and tell us how you get on. We can change the bookmarks around easily enough if you think<L.31.1>
you want different ones, or want them named differently etc. Let us know.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Online Games <C> Looking to the future, we need to get an idea of what competition we'd have if we rebuilt Gameplan as a truly<L.31.1>
interactive online game. What games do you guys know about, and what do you think of them? What can you find if you go out and<L.31.1>
look? What do you know about the companies already in the business of running games online, and how they operate? Who's good, and<L.31.1>
who's not? Note: by online we mean where you interact with your team directly online, rather than simply using the internet for<L.31.1>
sending stuff back and forth (as we're doing at present - we've only updated from play-by-mail to play-by-email).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports are now available for all games here. You should find PDF reports rather easier to cope<L.31.1>
with - Adobe Reader is free to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and you can open your reports with one click of the<L.31.1>
mouse (indeed, you don't need a printer, though most of you will then print from it) and you don't need to worry about dodgy email<L.31.1>
clients (Hotmail and AOL are particularly common culprits) messing up the formatting, or printer drivers. The text format for<L.31.1>
emailed reports is still available but I only expect people will want to do so if they use the text file for other purposes (such<L.31.1>
as exporting the listings into some software you've produced yourself).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
If you've not tried email reports before, or you've had problems, try out the PDF. It really is very straightforward.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Credit Card Payments <C> If you want to pay by credit card over the Internet you now have the option of paying in Sterling, US<L.31.1>
Dollars or Aussie Dollars, whichever you prefer. Cheques are still fine as well, and actually mean slightly lower charges for us!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Websites <C> The website for submitting orders is at www.softsim.co.uk. www.pbmsports.com is our main "static" information<L.31.1>
website, as well as news of what's going on here. For news of what is happening with Pete in Yeovil see www.sidetracks.co.uk. For<L.31.1>
information on baseball and how it works, see www.howbaseballworks.com - a site also designed for recruiting new punters!     <L.31.1>
